    & (<S: Object, T: Object>(s: S, t: T) => Merge3<
        // –í –∏—Ç–æ–≥–æ–≤–æ–º –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–µ –æ—Å—Ç–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ–ª—è –æ—Ç S, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –Ω–µ—Ç –≤ T

–î–∏–º, —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è –æ—á–µ—Ä–µ–¥—å, –Ω–æ—Ä–º?
export class Queue extends $.$mol_object2 {
    @mem tasks: $.$mol_atom2[] = []

    run(handler: () => void): void {
        this.tasks.push($.$mol_atom2_autorun(handler))
    }

    /**
        @return true if pending, false if complete, $.$mol_atom2 if error
     */
    get locked(): boolean | $.$mol_atom2 {
        if (this.tasks.length === 0) return

        const task = this.tasks[0]
        try {
            task.get()
            this.tasks = this.tasks.slice(1)
        } catch (error) {
            return task
        }

        return false
    }

    destructor() {
        super.destructor()
        const {tasks} = this
        for (let task of tasks) task.destructor()
        this.tasks = []
    }
}

Sergey Yuferev 
function createFiber(calculate: () => void): $.$mol_fiber {
    const fiber = new $.$mol_fiber
    fiber.calculate = calculate
    fiber[Symbol.toStringTag] = calculate.name

    return fiber
}

export class Queue extends $.$mol_object2 {
    @mem tasks: $.$mol_fiber[] = []

    run(calculate: () => void): void {
        this.tasks = [...this.tasks, createFiber(calculate)]
    }

    /**
        @return true if pending, false if complete, $.$mol_atom2 if error
     */
    get locked(): Error | PromiseLike<any> | void {
        if (this.tasks.length === 0) return

        const task = this.tasks[0]
        try {
            task.get()
            this.tasks = this.tasks.slice(1)
        } catch (error) {
            // Recreate fiber for future retry
            if (task.error) this.tasks[0] = createFiber(task.calculate)
            return error
        }
    }

    destructor() {
        super.destructor()
        const {tasks} = this
        for (let task of tasks) task.destructor()
        this.tasks = []
    }
}
